     ‚ē≠‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ēģ
     ‚Ēā Plan: failure policies (!policy) ‚ÄĒ replace proc!/contagion              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Context                                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā The proc! + whole-program can_panic contagion model (just built) is     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā heavier than arche needs.                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā After making most things total by construction (proven indexing,        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ok-valued insert, soon-clamped                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā slices), the residual set of operations that can fail at runtime is     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā tiny (~30 sites). So instead of                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā a propagation marker + call-graph effect analysis + (proposed)          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā recover/unwinding, we resolve each                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā failure locally, at the operation, by a policy ‚ÄĒ expr !policy. This     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā needs no unwinding, no                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā contagion, and gives a sharper guarantee than proc!: a func provably    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā never crashes; a proc                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā crashes only at a visible !abort site (marked at the line, not smeared  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā over the whole proc).                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ! is unified to mean "failure-handling policy" (generalizing proc!),    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā reusing the pool                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overload-policy idea from the original design discussion (Particle[100] ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !evict).                                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Locked decisions                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Replace proc! and the can_panic contagion pass entirely. Keep the     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā bounds prover                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (sem_bounds* in semantic.c) and the (h:, ok:) report form. No recover / ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā no stack unwinding.                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Every fallible op has a sensible DEFAULT policy (unannotated code     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā compiles); !policy                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overrides. LSP/analyzer hints surfacing the implicit policy are         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā mandatory.                                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - func = total policies only (can never crash). proc may also !abort.   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Slices default to !clamp; a provably-out-of-bounds constant           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā slice/index is a compile error                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (don't silently clamp a statically-wrong access).                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā The model                                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā expr !policy attaches a deterministic failure resolution at the site.   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Policies are total (op                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā cannot crash) except !abort (explicit, site-marked crash) and the (ok:) ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā report form.                                                            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒĆ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē¨‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē¨‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēź                                                                    ‚Ēā

     ‚Ēā ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēė                                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Proven safe (bounds prover) ‚áí raw access, no policy code at all.      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - func + !abort (explicit or as the would-be default) ‚áí compile error:  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā a func must prove it or                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā pick a total policy. (This is the one place a func "default" differs ‚ÄĒ  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā proposed func index default                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !clamp; confirm on review.)                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Pool layering: a pool decl sets the default (Particle[100] !evict); a ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā per-op !policy                                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overrides it.                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Phases                                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P1 ‚ÄĒ Parser: expr !policy                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Postfix !ident on index / slice / call expressions. ! already lexes as  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā TOK_BANG (Phase A). The                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policy ident becomes a leaf/child on the op node. Touch:                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā parser/parser.c (postfix-expr parsing for                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā SN_INDEX_EXPR / SN_SLICE_EXPR / SN_CALL/PROC_CALL). Remove the proc!    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā marker parse (Phase-A                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā parse_proc_marker-style !-after-proc), since proc! is gone.             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P2 ‚ÄĒ Remove proc! / contagion                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Delete: the can_panic/can_panic_marked fields (hir.h, sem_decls.h),     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā sem_check_panic_contagion                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā and the panic_walk/decl_body_panicky_callee helpers, E0095              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā panic_in_total, and the                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā analyzer proc! hint. Keep sem_bounds* (the prover) and bnd_* fact       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā machinery ‚ÄĒ repurposed:                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā "proven ‚áí no policy; unprovable ‚áí apply policy."                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P3 ‚ÄĒ Policy resolution (semantic)                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā For each fallible op: resolve policy = explicit !policy else            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā default(op-kind, pool-policy). Validate                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā func-total (no !abort in a func). Provable-OOB constant ‚áí error (reuse  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā bnd_lit_int + sized/min-len                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā facts). Attach the resolved policy to the op via a cst_id-keyed side    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā table (like the existing                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā sem_model side-model) so codegen reads it. Repurpose E0096 / add policy ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā diagnostics as needed.                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P4 ‚ÄĒ Codegen per policy                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā At each op, emit by resolved policy (replacing today's unconditional    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā check+abort):                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - index/slice !abort ‚Üí current                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā emit_bounds_check/emit_slice_bounds_check; !clamp ‚Üí min/max             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā clamp (slice) or clamped index; !zero ‚Üí in-bounds ? load : zero (skip   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā on write); !wrap ‚Üí                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā i % len.                                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - insert ‚Üí !abort (current overflow-abort), !reject (no-op + sentinel), ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā report (h:,ok:)                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (current mandatory-ok helper). !evict = ring cursor: pool gains one i64 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā head; on a full                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā insert do victim = head; head = (head+1) % cap; bump gen[victim] (same  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā gen-exhaustion check as                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā delete ‚ÄĒ this stales the evicted occupant's handle), overwrite          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā columns[victim], return                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (victim | gen<<32); count stays at cap, free-list untouched. O(1). ‚áí an ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !evict pool is for                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā anonymous streamed collectives, not rows you hold stable handles to.    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Implementation deferred                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā to a later milestone (adds the head field to the pool struct + the      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā full-path branch in the                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā insert helper), but the mechanism is fixed.                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - delete ‚Üí !abort (current stale-abort), report (ok:).                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - divide policies ‚ÄĒ defer (!abort only in v1, = current behavior).      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Touch: codegen/codegen.c (emit_bounds_check 4485,                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā emit_slice_bounds_check 1855, insert helper                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā 6859/overflow, delete helper 7026; index/slice/insert/delete call       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā lowering). Optional: elide policy                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā code when the prover proved the op safe (perf; deferrable ‚ÄĒ the         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā guarantee comes from func-total, not                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā from elision).                                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P5 ‚ÄĒ LSP hints (mandatory)                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Analyzer emits the implicit/explicit policy as an inlay at each         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā fallible op site. Reuse the                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā emit_effect_hint/emit_panic_hint infra in arche_analyzer.c ‚ÄĒ render     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā e.g. ghost !abort /                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !clamp after the op.                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā

     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā

     ‚Ēā adds head to the                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā pool struct), !wrap, divide policies, check elision.                    ‚Ēā

‚óŹ Both are important ‚ÄĒ and the first one actually forces a clarification in the
  model. Let me fold them in.

  The abort-guarantee surfaces a delete question: "never abort unless !abort"
  means the report form delete(h)(ok:) must be fully total ‚ÄĒ so a stale handle
  there returns ok=0, it does not abort. Only !abort (delete's default) aborts
  on stale. That refines the earlier "stale always aborts" rule into the
  unifying principle. Let me record all of it.

  ‚éŅ ¬†/plan to preview

‚óŹ Updated plan
  ‚éŅ ¬†/plan to preview

‚óŹ Both folded into the plan:

  - No-unexpected-abort guarantee tests ‚ÄĒ a policy/no_abort/ set with no !abort
  that triggers every failure condition through a total policy and asserts the
  program exits cleanly (&& %t). If anything aborts, the test fails. That's the
  guarantee, enforced. (Includes delete(stale)(ok:) ‚Üí ok=0, which also locked
  the clarification that the report form is fully total ‚ÄĒ only !abort aborts on
  stale.)
  - TODO: !evict_oldest (exact LRU via a per-row born-sequence column) ‚ÄĒ under a
  pay-per-policy metadata principle: a policy's extra per-pool metadata (the
  ring head, or the born-seq column) is compiled in only for pools that use that
  policy; everyone else pays nothing.

  The plan now covers the full !policy system, the abort guarantee + its tests,
  evict (ring cursor now, exact-oldest later), and the metadata principle.

     ‚ē≠‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ēģ
     ‚Ēā Plan: failure policies (!policy) ‚ÄĒ replace proc!/contagion              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Context                                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā The proc! + whole-program can_panic contagion model (just built) is     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā heavier than arche needs.                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā After making most things total by construction (proven indexing,        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ok-valued insert, soon-clamped                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā slices), the residual set of operations that can fail at runtime is     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā tiny (~30 sites). So instead of                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā a propagation marker + call-graph effect analysis + (proposed)          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā recover/unwinding, we resolve each                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā failure locally, at the operation, by a policy ‚ÄĒ expr !policy. This     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā needs no unwinding, no                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā contagion, and gives a sharper guarantee than proc!: a func provably    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā never crashes; a proc                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā crashes only at a visible !abort site (marked at the line, not smeared  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā over the whole proc).                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ! is unified to mean "failure-handling policy" (generalizing proc!),    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā reusing the pool                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overload-policy idea from the original design discussion (Particle[100] ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !evict).                                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Locked decisions                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Replace proc! and the can_panic contagion pass entirely. Keep the     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā bounds prover                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (sem_bounds* in semantic.c) and the (h:, ok:) report form. No recover / ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā no stack unwinding.                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Every fallible op has a sensible DEFAULT policy (unannotated code     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā compiles); !policy                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overrides. LSP/analyzer hints surfacing the implicit policy are         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā mandatory.                                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - func = total policies only (can never crash). proc may also !abort.   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Slices default to !clamp; a provably-out-of-bounds constant           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā slice/index is a compile error                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (don't silently clamp a statically-wrong access).                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā The model                                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā expr !policy attaches a deterministic failure resolution at the site.   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Policies are total (op                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā cannot crash) except !abort (explicit, site-marked crash) and the (ok:) ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā report form.                                                            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā

     ‚Ēā ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēė                                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Core guarantee: an op using anything other than !abort (a total policy, ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā or the report (ok:)                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā form) can never abort at runtime ‚ÄĒ period. This includes                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā delete(h)(ok:): a stale handle                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā there returns ok=0 (total), it does not abort. Only !abort (delete's    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā default) aborts on a stale                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā handle. (This refines the earlier "stale always aborts" decision: stale ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā aborts only under !abort.)                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Proven safe (bounds prover) ‚áí raw access, no policy code at all.      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - func + !abort (explicit or as the would-be default) ‚áí compile error:  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā a func must prove it or                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā pick a total policy. (This is the one place a func "default" differs ‚ÄĒ  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā proposed func index default                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !clamp; confirm on review.)                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Pool layering: a pool decl sets the default (Particle[100] !evict); a ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā per-op !policy                                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overrides it.                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Phases                                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P1 ‚ÄĒ Parser: expr !policy                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Postfix !ident on index / slice / call expressions. ! already lexes as  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā TOK_BANG (Phase A). The                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policy ident becomes a leaf/child on the op node. Touch:                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā parser/parser.c (postfix-expr parsing for                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā SN_INDEX_EXPR / SN_SLICE_EXPR / SN_CALL/PROC_CALL). Remove the proc!    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā marker parse (Phase-A                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā parse_proc_marker-style !-after-proc), since proc! is gone.             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P2 ‚ÄĒ Remove proc! / contagion                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Delete: the can_panic/can_panic_marked fields (hir.h, sem_decls.h),     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā sem_check_panic_contagion                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā and the panic_walk/decl_body_panicky_callee helpers, E0095              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā panic_in_total, and the                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā analyzer proc! hint. Keep sem_bounds* (the prover) and bnd_* fact       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā machinery ‚ÄĒ repurposed:                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā "proven ‚áí no policy; unprovable ‚áí apply policy."                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P3 ‚ÄĒ Policy resolution (semantic)                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā For each fallible op: resolve policy = explicit !policy else            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā default(op-kind, pool-policy). Validate                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā func-total (no !abort in a func). Provable-OOB constant ‚áí error (reuse  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā bnd_lit_int + sized/min-len                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā facts). Attach the resolved policy to the op via a cst_id-keyed side    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā table (like the existing                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā sem_model side-model) so codegen reads it. Repurpose E0096 / add policy ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā diagnostics as needed.                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P4 ‚ÄĒ Codegen per policy                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā At each op, emit by resolved policy (replacing today's unconditional    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā check+abort):                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - index/slice !abort ‚Üí current                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā emit_bounds_check/emit_slice_bounds_check; !clamp ‚Üí min/max             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā clamp (slice) or clamped index; !zero ‚Üí in-bounds ? load : zero (skip   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā on write); !wrap ‚Üí                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā i % len.                                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - insert ‚Üí !abort (current overflow-abort), !reject (no-op + sentinel), ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā report (h:,ok:)                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (current mandatory-ok helper). !evict = ring cursor: pool gains one i64 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā head; on a full                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā insert do victim = head; head = (head+1) % cap; bump gen[victim] (same  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā gen-exhaustion check as                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā delete ‚ÄĒ this stales the evicted occupant's handle), overwrite          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā columns[victim], return                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (victim | gen<<32); count stays at cap, free-list untouched. O(1). ‚áí an ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !evict pool is for                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā anonymous streamed collectives, not rows you hold stable handles to.    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Implementation deferred                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā to a later milestone (adds the head field to the pool struct + the      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā full-path branch in the                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā insert helper), but the mechanism is fixed.                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - delete ‚Üí !abort (current stale-abort), report (ok:).                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - divide policies ‚ÄĒ defer (!abort only in v1, = current behavior).      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Touch: codegen/codegen.c (emit_bounds_check 4485,                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā emit_slice_bounds_check 1855, insert helper                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā 6859/overflow, delete helper 7026; index/slice/insert/delete call       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā lowering). Optional: elide policy                                       ‚Ēā

‚óŹ That's the real generalization ‚ÄĒ policies should be user-definable, with the
  built-ins as shipped shorthand. This also forces a default flip: to honor
  "never abort unless !abort," the default policy must be total, so index/slice
  default to !clamp (not abort). Let me fold the framework into the plan.

‚óŹ Updated plan
  ‚éŅ ¬†/plan to preview

‚óŹ Updated plan
  ‚éŅ ¬†/plan to preview

‚óŹ Let me update the open-items list to reflect the resolved and new decisions,
  then re-present.

‚óŹ Updated plan  ‚éŅ ¬†/plan to preview

‚óŹ The plan now treats policies as user-definable funcs (per-category signature,
  invoked on the failure path), with the built-ins (clamp/wrap/evict/reject) as
  shipped shorthand over that mechanism, !abort/report as structural, a
  final-clamp safety net so even a custom policy can't abort (upholding the
  guarantee), and per-policy metadata compiled in only where used. Index/slice
  defaults flipped to !clamp to honor "no abort unless !abort." !evict_oldest
  becomes a library policy, not a built-in.

  A few defaults are genuinely undecided and flagged in the plan for review
  (notably insert/delete/divide have no clean silent total default; the fate of
  zero; user-policy signatures).
  ‚éŅ ¬†User rejected Claude's plan:
     ‚ē≠‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ēģ
     ‚Ēā Plan: failure policies (!policy) ‚ÄĒ replace proc!/contagion              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Context                                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā The proc! + whole-program can_panic contagion model (just built) is     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā heavier than arche needs.                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā After making most things total by construction (proven indexing,        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ok-valued insert, soon-clamped                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā slices), the residual set of operations that can fail at runtime is     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā tiny (~30 sites). So instead of                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā a propagation marker + call-graph effect analysis + (proposed)          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā recover/unwinding, we resolve each                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā failure locally, at the operation, by a policy ‚ÄĒ expr !policy. This     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā needs no unwinding, no                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā contagion, and gives a sharper guarantee than proc!: a func provably    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā never crashes; a proc                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā crashes only at a visible !abort site (marked at the line, not smeared  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā over the whole proc).                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ! is unified to mean "failure-handling policy" (generalizing proc!),    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā reusing the pool                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overload-policy idea from the original design discussion (Particle[100] ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !evict).                                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Locked decisions                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Replace proc! and the can_panic contagion pass entirely. Keep the     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā bounds prover                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (sem_bounds* in semantic.c) and the (h:, ok:) report form. No recover / ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā no stack unwinding.                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Every fallible op has a sensible DEFAULT policy (unannotated code     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā compiles); !policy                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overrides. LSP/analyzer hints surfacing the implicit policy are         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā mandatory.                                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - func = total policies only (can never crash). proc may also !abort.   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Slices default to !clamp; a provably-out-of-bounds constant           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā slice/index is a compile error                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (don't silently clamp a statically-wrong access).                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā The model                                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā expr !policy attaches a deterministic failure resolution at the site.   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Policies are total (op                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā cannot crash) except !abort (explicit, site-marked crash) and the (ok:) ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā report form.                                                            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒĆ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē¨‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē¨‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ ‚Ēā

     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒĒ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēī‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēī‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēė                                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Because the default must be total (no unexpected abort), index/slice    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā default to !clamp. !abort                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā is always opt-in. (Open: insert has no clean silent total default ‚ÄĒ     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !reject drops, !evict                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā destroys, report changes the call shape, !abort violates the guarantee  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ÄĒ so insert's default needs                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā a decision; same for delete/divide.)                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Core guarantee: an op using anything other than !abort (a total policy, ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā or the report (ok:)                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā form) can never abort at runtime ‚ÄĒ period. This includes                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā delete(h)(ok:): a stale handle                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā there returns ok=0 (total), it does not abort. Only !abort (delete's    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā default) aborts on a stale                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā handle. (This refines the earlier "stale always aborts" decision: stale ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā aborts only under !abort.)                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Proven safe (bounds prover) ‚áí raw access, no policy code at all.      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - func + !abort (explicit or as the would-be default) ‚áí compile error:  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā a func must prove it or                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā pick a total policy. (This is the one place a func "default" differs ‚ÄĒ  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā proposed func index default                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !clamp; confirm on review.)                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Pool layering: a pool decl sets the default (Particle[100] !evict); a ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā per-op !policy                                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overrides it.                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Policies are user-definable (built-ins are just shorthand)              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā A policy is an ordinary func invoked on the failure path, with a        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā signature fixed by the op                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā category; the built-ins (clamp, wrap, evict, reject) are predefined     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policy funcs in core/                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā stdlib. !name resolves to a policy func; a[i] !my_remap and insert(P,x) ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !my_evictor work the                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā same as the built-ins.                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Index/slice policy: func(len: int, i: int) -> int ‚Üí the index to use. ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā The language clamps                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā the returned index into [0, len) as a final net, so no policy (even a   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā buggy user one) can                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā cause an OOB ‚ÄĒ that's what makes "never abort unless !abort" hold for   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā arbitrary policies.                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Built-ins: clamp = identity-under-net, wrap = ((i%len)+len)%len.        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Pool-full policy: func(<pool ctx>) -> int ‚Üí the victim slot to        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overwrite, or -1 to reject.                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Built-ins: evict (ring: return+advance head), reject (-1). User         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policies = custom victim                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā selectors (oldest, lowest-priority, random) ‚ÄĒ this is how !evict_oldest ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā becomes a library                                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policy, not a compiler built-in.                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Structural built-ins (not funcs): !abort (opts OUT of the net ‚Üí       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā abort) and the report                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (h:, ok:) form (routes the failure to an out-param). These can't be     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā user funcs.                                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Constraints: a policy func must itself be total (no !abort inside) ‚ÄĒ  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā composes with the                                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā func-total rule; the final-clamp net covers correctness. A policy may   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā declare per-pool metadata                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā it needs (e.g. !evict_oldest's born-seq column), compiled into the pool ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā struct only for pools                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā that use it (pay-per-policy principle).                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - v1 ships the built-ins over this mechanism; the general user-policy   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā registration (resolving                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !name to a func, the per-category signature check, metadata             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā declaration) is the framework they                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā compile to ‚ÄĒ phase the public "define your own policy" surface after    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā the built-ins land.                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - zero (return the element's zero / skip write) doesn't fit the         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā index-remap shape ‚Üí keep it a                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā structural built-in, or drop it (open).                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Phases                                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P1 ‚ÄĒ Parser: expr !policy                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Postfix !ident on index / slice / call expressions. ! already lexes as  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā TOK_BANG (Phase A). The                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policy ident becomes a leaf/child on the op node. Touch:                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā parser/parser.c (postfix-expr parsing for                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā SN_INDEX_EXPR / SN_SLICE_EXPR / SN_CALL/PROC_CALL). Remove the proc!    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā marker parse (Phase-A                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā parse_proc_marker-style !-after-proc), since proc! is gone.             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P2 ‚ÄĒ Remove proc! / contagion                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Delete: the can_panic/can_panic_marked fields (hir.h, sem_decls.h),     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā sem_check_panic_contagion                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā and the panic_walk/decl_body_panicky_callee helpers, E0095              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā panic_in_total, and the                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā analyzer proc! hint. Keep sem_bounds* (the prover) and bnd_* fact       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā machinery ‚ÄĒ repurposed:                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā "proven ‚áí no policy; unprovable ‚áí apply policy."                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P3 ‚ÄĒ Policy resolution (semantic)                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā For each fallible op: resolve policy = explicit !policy else            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā default(op-kind, pool-policy). Validate                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā func-total (no !abort in a func). Provable-OOB constant ‚áí error (reuse  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā bnd_lit_int + sized/min-len                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā facts). Attach the resolved policy to the op via a cst_id-keyed side    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā table (like the existing                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā sem_model side-model) so codegen reads it. Repurpose E0096 / add policy ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā diagnostics as needed.                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P4 ‚ÄĒ Codegen per policy                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā At each op, emit by resolved policy (replacing today's unconditional    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā check+abort):                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - index/slice !abort ‚Üí current                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā emit_bounds_check/emit_slice_bounds_check; !clamp ‚Üí min/max             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā clamp (slice) or clamped index; !zero ‚Üí in-bounds ? load : zero (skip   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā on write); !wrap ‚Üí                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā i % len.                                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - insert ‚Üí !abort (current overflow-abort), !reject (no-op + sentinel), ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā report (h:,ok:)                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (current mandatory-ok helper). !evict = ring cursor: pool gains one i64 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā head; on a full                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā insert do victim = head; head = (head+1) % cap; bump gen[victim] (same  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā gen-exhaustion check as                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā delete ‚ÄĒ this stales the evicted occupant's handle), overwrite          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā columns[victim], return                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (victim | gen<<32); count stays at cap, free-list untouched. O(1). ‚áí an ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !evict pool is for                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā anonymous streamed collectives, not rows you hold stable handles to.    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Implementation deferred                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā to a later milestone (adds the head field to the pool struct + the      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā full-path branch in the                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā insert helper), but the mechanism is fixed.                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - delete ‚Üí !abort (current stale-abort), report (ok:).                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - divide policies ‚ÄĒ defer (!abort only in v1, = current behavior).      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Touch: codegen/codegen.c (emit_bounds_check 4485,                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā emit_slice_bounds_check 1855, insert helper                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā 6859/overflow, delete helper 7026; index/slice/insert/delete call       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā lowering). Optional: elide policy                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā code when the prover proved the op safe (perf; deferrable ‚ÄĒ the         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā guarantee comes from func-total, not                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā from elision).                                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P5 ‚ÄĒ LSP hints (mandatory)                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Analyzer emits the implicit/explicit policy as an inlay at each         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā fallible op site. Reuse the                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā emit_effect_hint/emit_panic_hint infra in arche_analyzer.c ‚ÄĒ render     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā e.g. ghost !abort /                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !clamp after the op.                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P6 ‚ÄĒ Migration                                                          ‚Ēā

     ‚Ēā - Keep the ~150 (h:, ok:) insert sites (report policy) and              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā delete(h)(ok:).                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - The defensive guards added in stdlib (str/csv/router/io) can be       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā simplified to proofs or policies                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā over time; not required for green.                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Scope / open items                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - v1 policies: !abort, !clamp, !zero (index/slice);                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !abort/!reject/report (insert);                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !abort/report (delete). Defer (mechanisms fixed): !evict (ring cursor ‚ÄĒ ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā adds head to the                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā pool struct), !wrap, divide policies, check elision.                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Pay-per-policy metadata principle: policy-specific per-pool metadata  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā is added to the pool                                                    ‚Ēā

     ‚Ēā head cursor only to                                                     ‚Ēā

     ‚Ēā policy declares the metadata it                                         ‚Ēā

‚óŹ Got it ‚ÄĒ I over-corrected. The guarantee is about the policy, not the default:
  !abort (whether implicit-default or explicit) is the only thing that can
  crash; any non-!abort policy never crashes, ever. So defaulting to !abort is
  totally fine. Let me fix that.

‚óŹ Updated plan
  ‚éŅ ¬†/plan to preview

‚óŹ Updated plan
  ‚éŅ ¬†/plan to preview

‚óŹ Fixed. Defaults are now !abort for procs (crash on the failure, just like
  today, surfaced by the LSP) / the matching total policy for funcs (which can't
  crash). The guarantee is purely about the policy: !abort ‚ÄĒ implicit or 
  explicit ‚ÄĒ is the only thing that can ever crash; every non-!abort policy is 
  crash-proof by construction (the final-clamp net guarantees it even for
  user-defined policies). The no_abort tests verify exactly that.

  The plan is consistent now: !policy system replacing proc!/contagion,
  user-definable policies with built-in shorthand, !abort-only crashing,
  ring-cursor !evict (+ !evict_oldest TODO with pay-per-policy metadata), the
  abort-guarantee tests, and a small set of flagged open items (fate of zero,
  single-index clamp semantics, exact user-policy signatures).
  ‚éŅ ¬†User rejected Claude's plan:
     ‚ē≠‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ēģ
     ‚Ēā Plan: failure policies (!policy) ‚ÄĒ replace proc!/contagion              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Context                                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā The proc! + whole-program can_panic contagion model (just built) is     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā heavier than arche needs.                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā After making most things total by construction (proven indexing,        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ok-valued insert, soon-clamped                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā slices), the residual set of operations that can fail at runtime is     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā tiny (~30 sites). So instead of                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā a propagation marker + call-graph effect analysis + (proposed)          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā recover/unwinding, we resolve each                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā failure locally, at the operation, by a policy ‚ÄĒ expr !policy. This     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā needs no unwinding, no                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā contagion, and gives a sharper guarantee than proc!: a func provably    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā never crashes; a proc                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā crashes only at a visible !abort site (marked at the line, not smeared  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā over the whole proc).                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ! is unified to mean "failure-handling policy" (generalizing proc!),    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā reusing the pool                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overload-policy idea from the original design discussion (Particle[100] ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !evict).                                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Locked decisions                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Replace proc! and the can_panic contagion pass entirely. Keep the     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā bounds prover                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (sem_bounds* in semantic.c) and the (h:, ok:) report form. No recover / ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā no stack unwinding.                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Every fallible op has a sensible DEFAULT policy (unannotated code     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā compiles); !policy                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overrides. LSP/analyzer hints surfacing the implicit policy are         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā mandatory.                                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - func = total policies only (can never crash). proc may also !abort.   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Slices default to !clamp; a provably-out-of-bounds constant           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā slice/index is a compile error                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (don't silently clamp a statically-wrong access).                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā The model                                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā expr !policy attaches a deterministic failure resolution at the site.   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Policies are total (op                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā cannot crash) except !abort (explicit, site-marked crash) and the (ok:) ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā report form.                                                            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒĆ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē¨‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē¨‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēź                                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā     op      ‚Ēā           policies           ‚Ēā   default (proc / func)  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§                                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā             ‚Ēā !clamp, !wrap, !zero,        ‚Ēā !abort / !clamp          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā index a[i]  ‚Ēā !abort, user policy          ‚Ēā (provable-OOB const ‚áí    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā             ‚Ēā                              ‚Ēā error)                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§                                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā slice       ‚Ēā                              ‚Ēā !abort / !clamp          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā a[x:y]      ‚Ēā !clamp, !abort, user policy  ‚Ēā (provable-OOB const ‚áí    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā             ‚Ēā                              ‚Ēā error)                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§                                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā             ‚Ēā !reject, !evict, !abort,     ‚Ēā pool's declared policy,  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā insert(P,x) ‚Ēā (h:, ok:) report, user       ‚Ēā else !abort              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā             ‚Ēā policy                       ‚Ēā                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§                                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā delete(h)   ‚Ēā !abort, (ok:) report         ‚Ēā !abort                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēú‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēľ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ē§                                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ēā a / b       ‚Ēā !zero, !wrap, !abort         ‚Ēā !abort / !zero           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   ‚Ēā                                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒĒ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēī‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēī‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚Ēė                                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā The guarantee is about the policy, not the default: !abort ‚ÄĒ whether    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā it's the implicit                                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā default or explicitly written ‚ÄĒ is the only thing that can crash. Any   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā non-!abort policy                                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (default or explicit) never crashes, in theory, ever. So defaulting a   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā proc op to !abort is fine                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (unannotated code crashes on the failure, exactly like today; the LSP   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā hint surfaces the implicit                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !abort). A func can't use !abort (funcs stay crash-proof), so its       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā default is the relevant                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā total policy (!clamp for index/slice, !zero for divide) ‚ÄĒ still no      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā compile error, just a                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā total default. Writing any explicit total policy (!clamp, !reject,      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā report, ‚Ä¶) guarantees no                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā crash.                                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Core guarantee: an op using anything other than !abort (a total policy, ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā or the report (ok:)                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā form) can never abort at runtime ‚ÄĒ period. This includes                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā delete(h)(ok:): a stale handle                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā there returns ok=0 (total), it does not abort. Only !abort (delete's    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā default) aborts on a stale                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā handle. (This refines the earlier "stale always aborts" decision: stale ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā aborts only under !abort.)                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Proven safe (bounds prover) ‚áí raw access, no policy code at all.      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - func + !abort (explicit or as the would-be default) ‚áí compile error:  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā a func must prove it or                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā pick a total policy. (This is the one place a func "default" differs ‚ÄĒ  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā proposed func index default                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !clamp; confirm on review.)                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Pool layering: a pool decl sets the default (Particle[100] !evict); a ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā per-op !policy                                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overrides it.                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Policies are user-definable (built-ins are just shorthand)              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā A policy is an ordinary func invoked on the failure path, with a        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā signature fixed by the op                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā category; the built-ins (clamp, wrap, evict, reject) are predefined     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policy funcs in core/                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā stdlib. !name resolves to a policy func; a[i] !my_remap and insert(P,x) ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !my_evictor work the                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā same as the built-ins.                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Index/slice policy: func(len: int, i: int) -> int ‚Üí the index to use. ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā The language clamps                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā the returned index into [0, len) as a final net, so no policy (even a   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā buggy user one) can                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā cause an OOB ‚ÄĒ that's what makes "never abort unless !abort" hold for   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā arbitrary policies.                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Built-ins: clamp = identity-under-net, wrap = ((i%len)+len)%len.        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Pool-full policy: func(<pool ctx>) -> int ‚Üí the victim slot to        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā overwrite, or -1 to reject.                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Built-ins: evict (ring: return+advance head), reject (-1). User         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policies = custom victim                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā selectors (oldest, lowest-priority, random) ‚ÄĒ this is how !evict_oldest ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā becomes a library                                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policy, not a compiler built-in.                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Structural built-ins (not funcs): !abort (opts OUT of the net ‚Üí       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā abort) and the report                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (h:, ok:) form (routes the failure to an out-param). These can't be     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā user funcs.                                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Constraints: a policy func must itself be total (no !abort inside) ‚ÄĒ  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā composes with the                                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā func-total rule; the final-clamp net covers correctness. A policy may   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā declare per-pool metadata                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā it needs (e.g. !evict_oldest's born-seq column), compiled into the pool ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā struct only for pools                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā that use it (pay-per-policy principle).                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - v1 ships the built-ins over this mechanism; the general user-policy   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā registration (resolving                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !name to a func, the per-category signature check, metadata             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā declaration) is the framework they                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā compile to ‚ÄĒ phase the public "define your own policy" surface after    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā the built-ins land.                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - zero (return the element's zero / skip write) doesn't fit the         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā index-remap shape ‚Üí keep it a                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā structural built-in, or drop it (open).                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Phases                                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P1 ‚ÄĒ Parser: expr !policy                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Postfix !ident on index / slice / call expressions. ! already lexes as  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā TOK_BANG (Phase A). The                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policy ident becomes a leaf/child on the op node. Touch:                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā parser/parser.c (postfix-expr parsing for                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā SN_INDEX_EXPR / SN_SLICE_EXPR / SN_CALL/PROC_CALL). Remove the proc!    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā marker parse (Phase-A                                                   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā parse_proc_marker-style !-after-proc), since proc! is gone.             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P2 ‚ÄĒ Remove proc! / contagion                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Delete: the can_panic/can_panic_marked fields (hir.h, sem_decls.h),     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā sem_check_panic_contagion                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā and the panic_walk/decl_body_panicky_callee helpers, E0095              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā panic_in_total, and the                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā analyzer proc! hint. Keep sem_bounds* (the prover) and bnd_* fact       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā machinery ‚ÄĒ repurposed:                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā "proven ‚áí no policy; unprovable ‚áí apply policy."                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P3 ‚ÄĒ Policy resolution (semantic)                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā For each fallible op: resolve policy = explicit !policy else            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā default(op-kind, pool-policy). Validate                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā func-total (no !abort in a func). Provable-OOB constant ‚áí error (reuse  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā bnd_lit_int + sized/min-len                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā facts). Attach the resolved policy to the op via a cst_id-keyed side    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā table (like the existing                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā sem_model side-model) so codegen reads it. Repurpose E0096 / add policy ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā diagnostics as needed.                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P4 ‚ÄĒ Codegen per policy                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā At each op, emit by resolved policy (replacing today's unconditional    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā check+abort):                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - index/slice !abort ‚Üí current                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā emit_bounds_check/emit_slice_bounds_check; !clamp ‚Üí min/max             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā clamp (slice) or clamped index; !zero ‚Üí in-bounds ? load : zero (skip   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā on write); !wrap ‚Üí                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā i % len.                                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - insert ‚Üí !abort (current overflow-abort), !reject (no-op + sentinel), ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā report (h:,ok:)                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (current mandatory-ok helper). !evict = ring cursor: pool gains one i64 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā head; on a full                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā insert do victim = head; head = (head+1) % cap; bump gen[victim] (same  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā gen-exhaustion check as                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā delete ‚ÄĒ this stales the evicted occupant's handle), overwrite          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā columns[victim], return                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (victim | gen<<32); count stays at cap, free-list untouched. O(1). ‚áí an ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !evict pool is for                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā anonymous streamed collectives, not rows you hold stable handles to.    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Implementation deferred                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā to a later milestone (adds the head field to the pool struct + the      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā full-path branch in the                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā insert helper), but the mechanism is fixed.                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - delete ‚Üí !abort (current stale-abort), report (ok:).                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - divide policies ‚ÄĒ defer (!abort only in v1, = current behavior).      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Touch: codegen/codegen.c (emit_bounds_check 4485,                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā emit_slice_bounds_check 1855, insert helper                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā 6859/overflow, delete helper 7026; index/slice/insert/delete call       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā lowering). Optional: elide policy                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā code when the prover proved the op safe (perf; deferrable ‚ÄĒ the         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā guarantee comes from func-total, not                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā from elision).                                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P5 ‚ÄĒ LSP hints (mandatory)                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Analyzer emits the implicit/explicit policy as an inlay at each         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā fallible op site. Reuse the                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā emit_effect_hint/emit_panic_hint infra in arche_analyzer.c ‚ÄĒ render     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā e.g. ghost !abort /                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !clamp after the op.                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā P6 ‚ÄĒ Migration                                                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Remove the 3 proc! panic tests; convert                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā panic_in_total/insert_delete_outlist tests.                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - *_array_oob tests ‚Üí default !abort ‚áí revert to runtime-abort          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā assertions (or !abort explicit).                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - slice_oob_rejected ‚Üí !clamp default (no abort) + a provable-OOB-const ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā compile-error test.                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Keep the ~150 (h:, ok:) insert sites (report policy) and              ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā delete(h)(ok:).                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - The defensive guards added in stdlib (str/csv/router/io) can be       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā simplified to proofs or policies                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā over time; not required for green.                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Scope / open items                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - v1 policies: !abort, !clamp, !zero (index/slice);                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !abort/!reject/report (insert);                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !abort/report (delete). Defer (mechanisms fixed): !evict (ring cursor ‚ÄĒ ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā adds head to the                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā pool struct), !wrap, divide policies, check elision.                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Pay-per-policy metadata principle: policy-specific per-pool metadata  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā is added to the pool                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā struct only when that pool actually uses the policy ‚ÄĒ !evict adds the   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā head cursor only to                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā !evict pools; ordinary pools pay nothing. Generalize this so each       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policy declares the metadata it                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā needs and it's compiled in per-pool on demand.                          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - TODO ‚ÄĒ !evict_oldest (exact LRU-by-age): a future eviction policy     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā that removes the truly                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā oldest row (not ring round-robin), via a per-row born-sequence column.  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā It MAY add that column ‚ÄĒ                                                ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā but only for pools compiled with this specific policy (per the          ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā principle above); pools using                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā plain !evict or no eviction never carry it. Evaluate min-via-scan vs a  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā min-heap when built.                                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Open decisions:                                                       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   - Fate of zero (structural built-in vs drop) ‚ÄĒ doesn't fit the        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā index-remap func shape.                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   - Single-index !clamp read/write semantics (read = a[clamp(i)]; write ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā = clamp target).                                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   - User-policy framework: exact per-category signatures + how a policy ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā declares per-pool metadata.                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā   - (Resolved: defaults are !abort for procs / the matching total       ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā policy for funcs; only !abort                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā can crash.)                                                             ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā Verification                                                            ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā                                                                         ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - Clean make all (no -Werror warnings); make test (535+), doctests,     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā make verify-syntax.                                                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - New tests under tests/unit/language/policy/: each v1 policy on index  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā + slice + insert; func                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā rejecting !abort; provable-OOB constant ‚áí compile error; default-policy ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā behavior; analyzer dump                                                 ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā shows the implicit-policy inlay.                                        ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā - No-unexpected-abort guarantee tests (required). A                     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā tests/unit/language/policy/no_abort/                                    ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā set: programs that contain no !abort and deliberately trigger every     ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā failure condition through                                               ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā a total policy, asserting the program runs to completion / exits 0      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā (i.e. RUN ‚Ä¶ && %t, not                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā ‚Ä¶ && ! %t). At minimum: a[oob] !clamp, a[oob] !zero, a[lo:huge] !clamp, ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā insert into a                                                           ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā full pool with !reject (and !evict once built), and delete(stale)(ok:)  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā returning ok=0. If                                                      ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā any of these aborts, the test fails ‚ÄĒ that's the guarantee. (Mirror of  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā the *_array_oob tests,                                                  ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā inverted: those assert !abort does abort; these assert total policies   ‚Ēā
     ‚Ēā never do.)                                                              ‚Ēā
     ‚ēį‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ‚ēĮ

‚óŹ Here's the proposed syntax. A policy sits in arche's unified name :: <form>
  grammar (alongside proc/func/sys) as a policy form, referenced with !name. Its
  signature shape picks the op category; the body must be total; built-ins are
  just policies shipped in core.

  // ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ INDEX / SLICE policy: (len, requested i) -> index to use.
  //    The language final-clamps the result into [0, len), so a policy can
  never cause an OOB.
  clamp :: policy(len: int, i: int) -> int {
    if (i < 0)    { return 0; }
    if (i >= len) { return len - 1; }
    return i;
  }
  wrap :: policy(len: int, i: int) -> int {
    return ((i % len) + len) % len;
  }

  v := samples[k] !wrap;      // read, wrapped into range
  grid[x] !clamp = c;         // write, clamped

  // ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ POOL-FULL policy: pick a victim slot, or -1 to reject.
  //    `uses { ‚Ä¶ }` declares per-pool metadata, compiled into the pool struct
  ONLY for
  //    pools that use this policy (pay-per-policy ‚ÄĒ ordinary pools carry
  nothing).
  reject :: policy(cap: int) -> int { return 0 - 1; }

  evict :: policy(cap: int) -> int  uses { head: i64 } {   // ring
    v := head;
    head = (head + 1) % cap;
    return v;
  }

  Particle[1000] !evict            // pool's default policy
  insert(Particle, p)              // uses the pool default (!evict)
  insert(Particle, p) !abort       // per-op override

  // ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ DIVIDE policy: (a, b) -> result, invoked when b == 0.
  zero :: policy(a: int, b: int) -> int { return 0; }
  r := n / d !zero;

  // ‚ĒÄ‚ĒÄ A custom policy is just another `policy` decl, used the same way:
  nearest :: policy(len: int, i: int) -> int { if (i < 0) { return 0; } if (i >=
  len) { return len - 1; } return i; }
  Enemies[256] !my_evictor         // any user pool policy
  hp := stats[idx] !nearest;

  Structural built-ins (NOT user policies) ‚ÄĒ !abort (opts out of the net ‚Üí
  crash) and the report form insert(P,p)(h:, ok:) / delete(h)(ok:) (failure as a
  value).

  Two things this surfaces:
  - Empty-array edge: when len == 0 no policy can return a valid index, so the
  net resolves it (read ‚Üí element's zero, write ‚Üí skip) ‚ÄĒ still no abort.
  - Stateful pool policies like evict_oldest need bookkeeping on every insert
  (stamp a born-seq), not just on the full-path victim pick ‚ÄĒ so a pool policy
  is really two hooks: an optional on_insert(slot) and the select_victim(cap) ->
  slot|-1. The ring evict only needs the victim hook; evict_oldest needs both.
  I'll spec that two-hook interface in the framework.

  Let me record this in the plan.

‚óŹ Updated plan
  ‚éŅ ¬†/plan to preview

‚óŹ Shown above and recorded in the plan (the policy form, !name usage, uses { ‚Ä¶ }
  per-pool metadata, the index/pool/divide categories, the empty-array net, and
  the two-hook pool interface for stateful policies like evict_oldest).

  The plan now fully specifies: !policy replacing proc!/contagion;
  user-definable policies (policy form) with built-in shorthand; !abort as the
  sole crashing policy (default for procs, total default for funcs); the
  final-clamp net guaranteeing non-!abort policies never crash; ring-cursor
  !evict + !evict_oldest TODO; the abort-guarantee tests; and the flagged open
  items (fate of zero, single-index clamp semantics, exact user-policy
  signatures + two-hook pool interface).
